Pratical case  with a combination of CTE and Row_number()

I had seven tables to join and a lot of rules to apply until get the final recordset, and the most 
complex part was based in the rules I needed to get the record before ... 

to get the right data I used Common Table Expressions CTE and  ROW_NUMBER() function.

I leave you a sample How to combine this two SQl Server commands to filter through a range of Data

##  1. Create and Populate tables with values


* Create tables 


<pre><code>IF OBJECT_ID ('Message_Operators','U') IS NOT NULL
DROP TABLE Message_Operators;
GO 

CREATE TABLE Message_Operators (

		[Id]         [smallint]  NOT NULL,  
		[Code]       [char](4) ,
		[Name]       [varchar](25) 
		 PRIMARY KEY ([Id])
)


IF OBJECT_ID ('Message_Types','U') IS NOT NULL
    DROP TABLE Message_Types;
GO 


CREATE TABLE Message_Types (
	    [Id]           [smallint]  NOT NULL,  
		[Message_Type] [varchar](25) 
		 PRIMARY KEY ([Id])
)
GO 


IF OBJECT_ID ('Message_Data','U') IS NOT NULL
    DROP TABLE Message_Data;
GO 

CREATE TABLE Message_Data (
		[Id]                 [bigint]  PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY (1, 1),
		[Identifier]         [varchar] (26) not NULL,
		[Message_Type_Id]    [smallint] ,
		[Body]               [varchar] (8000) NULL,
	    [Sender_ID]          [smallint] NULL,
		[Receiver_ID]        [smallint] NULL,
		[Date_Created]       [datetime2](3) NOT NULL
		FOREIGN KEY ([Message_Type_Id]) REFERENCES Message_Types ([Id]),
		FOREIGN KEY ([Sender_ID]) REFERENCES Message_Operators ([Id]),
		FOREIGN KEY ([Receiver_ID]) REFERENCES Message_Operators ([Id])
	)

GO 
</code></pre>


* Populate Tables 


<pre><code>Insert into  Message_Operators([Id]  , [Code] , [Name] ) 
VALUES

GO 


Insert into  Message_Types([Id]  , [Message_Type] ) 
VALUES
(1, 'Type_1'),

GO 
</code></pre>

## 2 - Pratical case
 
* assigns a sequential number break by partition Identifier

I have three tables related with one message system
+ Message_Operators correspond to  Senders and Receivers 
+ Message_Types 
+ Message_Data  has a unique identifier a message type a Sender and a Receiver

Goal : 
In the Message_Data table, you can have several messages for the same unique identifier.
Given a Type of message give the message before, don't forget a message can have the same type more than one time and you need to give all the messages before. 

To get the right data I used Common Table Expressions CTE and  ROW_NUMBER() function.

I leave you a sample How to combine these two SQL Server commands to filter through the range of Data.

<pre><code>
Declare @message_type varchar(10)
Set @message_type = 'Type_10'

;WITH CTE_tb1 AS (
Select md.Id, md.Identifier,  mt.Message_Type, mos.code As Sender, mor.Code as Receiver 
,     ROW_NUMBER() over (partition by Identifier order by md.ID    ) as RowNumber1ASC 
from dbo.Message_data md
inner join dbo.Message_Types mt     on md.Message_type_id = mt.id
inner join dbo.Message_Operators mos on md.Sender_ID = mos.id
inner join dbo.Message_Operators mor on md.Receiver_ID = mor.id
), CTE_tb2 AS (
   Select Id, Identifier, Message_Type, Sender, Receiver, RowNumber1ASC
   from CTE_tb1
   Where Message_Type = @message_type
)
Select tb1.Identifier, tb1.Message_Type, tb1.Sender, tb1.Receiver, tb1.RowNumber1ASC
from CTE_tb2 tb2
inner join CTE_tb1 tb1  ON tb2.Identifier = tb1.Identifier
Where tb1.RowNumber1ASC = tb2.RowNumber1ASC -1 
</code></pre>
